msg:I originally planned to stay in Jinan for three days, but the weather forecast said it would snow heavily. Since I was driving by myself, I had to return early. I am from Qingdao, and you know the relationship between Qingdao and Jinan üòè, but I want to say that I felt really good during the few days I stayed in this hotel. First of all, the lady at the front desk was very enthusiastic. When our family came, the security guard at the door specially pulled a luggage cart to carry our luggage and sent it upstairs. We also had a room upgrade service for an extra dollar. We upgraded it immediately after mentioning it. As soon as we got out of the elevator door, there were fruits and mineral water in the corridor. We could take them at will. We upgraded to a luxury big bed, which felt like a suite, but the view outside the window was not very beautiful because they were dismantling something. However, the room was very quiet, and the sound outside was basically inaudible. The room also prepared earplugs, and the whole room was controlled by Xiaodu, but the TV could not be connected, and everything else was very sensitive. Because we were out during these few days, we didn't experience their gym and afternoon tea, but we went to have breakfast. The breakfast variety is very rich, and the most important thing is that you can order it a la carte. They can make seafood porridge freshly, and the taste is very good. Because we are driving ourselves, we don't consider traffic problems. I feel very convinced here for these two days. You can park anywhere in the parking lot. There are plenty of spaces on the ground and underground. It is only 20 minutes away from Baotu Spring, which is very convenient. There are robots to deliver takeout to you. You have to swipe the room card to go upstairs, otherwise the elevator will not work. If there is a problem, the front desk will almost reply in seconds. I will continue to stay here for a few more days if I have the chance. By the way, Chaos is not bad either.
